

```python
# Dependencies
from citipy import citipy
import requests as req
import json
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import pandas as pd
import seaborn as sns
from random import randrange
import openweathermapy as ow
%matplotlib inline
```


```python
#Api key and url for open weather map
api_key = "6ebf95dafbd1ab39b94597759c533e9d"
```


```python
#Randomly selected the longitude and latitude
city_dict = {}
weather_data = []
count = 0
while count < 500:
    lat = randrange(-90, 90)
    lng = randrange(-180, 180)
    location = citipy.nearest_city(lat, lng)
    city = location.city_name
    country = location.country_code
    if not city in city_dict:
        city_dict.update({city:country})
        url = 'http://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?q={},{}&units=Imperial&APPID={}'.format(city, country, api_key)
        response = req.get(url).json()
        if response != {'cod': '404', 'message': 'city not found'}:
            #print(url)
            weather_data.append(response)
            count = len(weather_data)
print(weather_data)
```

```python
## Instructions ##
# Randomly select at least 500 unique (non-repeat) cities based on latitude and longitude.
# Perform a weather check on each of the cities using a series of successive API calls.
# Include a print log of each city as it's being processed with the city number, city name, and requested URL.
# Save both a CSV of all data retrieved and png images for each scatter plot.
# Temperature (F) vs. Latitude
# Humidity (%) vs. Latitude
# Cloudiness (%) vs. Latitude
# Wind Speed (mph) vs. Latitude
```


```python
lat_data = [data.get("coord").get("lat") for data in weather_data]
temp_data = [data.get("main").get("temp_max") for data in weather_data]
lon_data = [data.get("coord").get("lon") for data in weather_data]
humid_data = [data.get("main").get("humidity") for data in weather_data]
wind_spd = [data.get("wind").get("speed") for data in weather_data]
cloud_data = [data.get("clouds").get("all") for data in weather_data]
city_data = [data.get("name") for data in weather_data]
date_data = [data.get("dt") for data in weather_data]
weather_df = pd.DataFrame({"City": city_data,
                    "Latitude": lat_data,
                    "Temperature (F)": temp_data,
                    "Longitude": lon_data,
                    "Humidity": humid_data,
                    "Wind Speed": wind_spd,
                    "Cloudiness": cloud_data,
                    "Date": date_data})
weather_df.head()

```

```python
# Temperature (F) vs. Latitude Scatter Plot
sns.regplot(x=weather_df["Latitude"], y=weather_df["Temperature (F)"], fit_reg=False) 
plt.legend()
# Titles and grids
plt.title("City Latitude vs Max Temperature")
plt.xlabel("Latitude")
plt.ylabel("Max Temperature (F)")
# Bottom Label
plt.figtext(1,0.8, "Note: Cities at higher latitudes experience lower temperatures.", fontsize=9)
# Print Scatter Plot
plt.show()

```


![png](output_6_0.png)



```python
# Humidity vs. Latitude Scatter Plot
sns.regplot(x=weather_df["Latitude"], y=weather_df["Humidity"], fit_reg=False) 
plt.legend()
# Titles and grids
plt.title("City Latitude vs Humidity")
plt.xlabel("Latitude")
plt.ylabel("Humidity")
# Bottom Label
plt.figtext(1,0.8, "Note: There is no correlation between latitude and humidity. ", fontsize=9)
# Print Scatter Plot
plt.show()
```


![png](output_7_0.png)



```python
# Cloudiness vs. Latitude Scatter Plot
sns.regplot(x=weather_df["Latitude"], y=weather_df["Cloudiness"], fit_reg=False) 
plt.legend()
# Titles and grids
plt.title("City Latitude vs Cloudiness")
plt.xlabel("Latitude")
plt.ylabel("Cloudiness (%)")
# Bottom Label
plt.figtext(1,0.8, "Note: There is no correlation between cloudiness and latitude. ", fontsize=9)
# Print Scatter Plot
plt.show()
```

plt.ylabel("Wind Speed")
